(PID.TID 0000.0001) ># This is an additional Leith Viscosity, prop to grad(div.v_h)
(PID.TID 0000.0001) ># It traps instabilities that have no signal in grad(curl v_h)
(PID.TID 0000.0001) ># viscC2leithD=5.,
